 Let us know the similarities between the two leaders
 1
 Pandit Nehru was the first major electoral face of the Congress
 party ne unke naam or kaam, donon kaa istemaal vot batorne ke liye kiya

 2
 Nehru was identified as a world leader with his imprint on foreign policy
 unki nijee soch kii chhap tatkaaleen sarkaar kii videsh nitiyon main saaf jhalkati
